name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Club Partial River View Twin Room,2 Twin Beds, Non-smoking

posted:Posted May 21, 2024
msg:1. A small shop selling Maotai has been newly added on the left hand side of the entrance. This kind of setting has been seen in some five-star hotels in fifth-tier cities, but it is generally limited to high-end fashion shoes and bags and other goods that are needed for emergency evening parties. What the Westin Hotel guests need in an emergency is Maotai?
2. When queuing, guests cut in line at will. The front desk does not maintain order. It is not like a five-star hotel at all. After complaining, I initially thought that I would not deal with it. I waited for half an hour at the front desk. Finally, I got an apology from the duty manager. They said that they would strengthen training. It is not easy for guests to rush to promote businesses to improve their service level.
3. Breakfast was not finished. No matter the "occupancy" nameplate, full cup of coffee and full plate of fruit, the meal was taken away within a minute after the person left to get the food. After pointing it out, the two waiters left without saying a word... I had to politely ask them to come back and trouble them to help bring back some fruit. After a while, two lonely pears came back and said that the other fruits had been thrown away. So they were in a hurry to collect the meal and take out the garbage instead of thinking about serving the guests who really need it?
4. The restaurant faces the garden. You can see that the cleaning staff of the garden building are not equipped with special cleaning buckets and basins. Are the rags washed in the fountain?
5. When breakfast was almost over, the waiter quarreled loudly in front of the guests and almost got into a fight. The guests who were sipping coffee nearby immediately put down their cups and left the restaurant. Low management level
6. We booked a river view room, but it turned out to be the side of the building. We saw a line of river view. We asked the front desk and found out that it was called side river view. But the side view was not even as good as the ordinary room because the residents of the high-rise building opposite had clothes hanging on the balconies. The ordinary rooms at the back at least had a view of the garden at the back of the hotel. What's worse is that there was municipal construction downstairs. On Saturday, it kept banging until 1 a.m. The hotel notice said it started two years ago. The hotel should know about this noise pollution. In this case, they still marked the side rooms as side river view and charged half the price. I can only say that the management awareness of Wuhan Westin is low. It's the level of killing chickens to get * when you look "forward"
I came to Wuhan Westin ten years ago and had a good impression. I was very disappointed this time. I quickly changed to Donghu. No matter how good the location is, it will only sink without good management. Wuhan Westin, never see you again
